Forums : Openremote Controller not opening
This page last changed on Nov 25, 2011 by williammanda.

I installed the Openremote controller file: Openremote-Controller-2.0.0_SNAPSHOT_20110611. I then started the program in terminal in the /bin directory with: ./openremote.sh run. I then opened a browser with: http://localhost:8080/controller. I get the login screen and enter my user name and password but the controller gui doesn't come up. I get a changed login screen:

I created an account for the Openremote Boss 2.0 online tools. Created a device and android panel for my phone to control Mythtv via telnet which works.

My system:
Ubuntu 11.10 32 bit
The java version result:

java version "1.6.0_26"
